<!--this  document用于保存程序 of 清理规则-->
<Data>
  <CleanCollection4>
    <!--Expired documents-->
    <Item Name="#Superseded WinSxS components" Level="2">
      <Description>#清理被取代 of 组件并减少组件 storage of 大小. </Description>
      <Group>#Expired documents</Group>
      <ScanCollection>
        <!--exist 这里填写扫描规则，Dism++Will 自动匹配第一条命中 of 规则-->
        
        <!--Vista~Windows 8.1-->
        <Scan Work="15">
          <Applicable>
            <OSVersion Compare="&lt;">10.0</OSVersion>
          </Applicable>
          <Warning>#Updates cannot be uninstalled after cleaning，Do not use this option if you need to uninstall updates. </Warning>
          <Activate>
            <Custom ProcName="DismComponentCleanup" Flags="#1"/>
          </Activate>
        </Scan>
        
        <!--Windows 10exist 线-->
        <Scan Work="15">
          <Applicable>
            <OSVersion Compare=">=">10.0</OSVersion>
            <ImageFlags>1</ImageFlags>
          </Applicable>
          <Warning>#Updates cannot be uninstalled after cleaning，In addition, the ResetBase mode conflicts with the system reset function.，Do not use this option if you need to uninstall updates or reset the system.. </Warning>
          <Activate>
            <Custom ProcName="DismComponentCleanup" Flags="#1"/>
          </Activate>
        </Scan>
        
        <!--Windows 10离线，因为离线not 能重启避免一些麻烦，离线下closure Resetbase-->
        <Scan Work="50">
          <Name>#Superseded WinSxS components（Very Slow）</Name>
          <Applicable>
            <OSVersion Compare=">=">10.0</OSVersion>
            <Not>
              <ImageFlags>1</ImageFlags>
            </Not>
          </Applicable>
          <Warning>#Updates cannot be uninstalled after cleaning，Do not use this option if you need to uninstall updates. </Warning>
          <Activate>
            <Custom ProcName="DismComponentCleanup"/>
          </Activate>
        </Scan>
      </ScanCollection>
    </Item>

    <Item Name="#以前 of Windows system " Level="2">
      <Description>#exist  system 升级or还原后留下 of  system 备份. </Description>
      <Warning>#删除后你Will Unable to 回滚 arrive 以前安装 of  system . </Warning>
      <Group>#Expired documents</Group>
      <Scan Work="5">
        <Applicable>
          <FileExist FilePath="%SystemDrive%\Windows.old"/>
        </Applicable>
        <Activate>
          <General RootPath="%SystemDrive%" Flags="Directory">
            <Query>Windows.old*</Query>
          </General>
        </Activate>
      </Scan>
    </Item>

    <Item Name="#以前 of Dism++组件" Level="3">

      <Group>#Expired documents</Group>
      <Scan>

        <Activate>
          <General RootPath="%0%Config\">
            <Query>wsusscn2.cab.Session</Query>
            <Query>DismRule.xml</Query>
            <Query>Dism.xml</Query>
            <Query>Config*</Query>
            <Excluded>Config.ini</Excluded>
          </General>
          <General RootPath="%0%Config\amd64">
            <Query>BCDBoot</Query>
            <Query>DuiLib.dll</Query>
            <Query>Plug-in</Query>
            <Query>nativedism.exe</Query>
            <Query>Dism</Query>
          </General>
          <General RootPath="%0%Config\x86">
            <Query>BCDBoot</Query>
            <Query>DuiLib.dll</Query>
            <Query>Plug-in</Query>
            <Query>nativedism.exe</Query>
            <Query>Dism</Query>
          </General>
          <General RootPath="%0%Config\Languages">
            <Excluded>?GetLocaleName().zip</Excluded>
          </General>
          <General RootPath="%0%Config\Plugins" Flags="Directory">
            <Query>{*}</Query>
          </General>
          <General RootPath="%0%">
            <Query>*.dmp</Query>
            <Query>What's New(beta).txt</Query>
            <Query>What's New(Public).txt</Query>
          </General>
        </Activate>
      </Scan>

    <Item Name="#Chrome浏览器老版versions 备份（by Honry）" Level="2">
      <!--2016-04-08 14:43添加-->
      <Description>#Chrome浏览器升级 arrive 新版versions 后留下 of Backing up files，Roll back to the old version in case of failure. </Description>
      <Group>#Expired documents</Group>
      <Scan>
        <Applicable>
          <ImageFlags>1</ImageFlags>
          <Or>
            <RegExist Key="HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\App Paths\chrome.exe" Value="Path"/>
            <RegExist Key="HKLM\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\App Paths\chrome.exe" Value="Path"/>
          </Or>
        </Applicable>
        <Applicable_1>
          <RegExist Key="HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\App Paths\chrome.exe" Value="Path"/>
          <Not>
            <FileExist FilePath="?GetRegSz(HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\App Paths\chrome.exe,Path)\new_chrome.exe"/>
          </Not>
        </Applicable_1>
        <Applicable_2>
          <RegExist Key="HKLM\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\App Paths\chrome.exe" Value="Path"/>
          <Not>
            <FileExist FilePath="?GetRegSz(HKLM\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\App Paths\chrome.exe,Path)\new_chrome.exe"/>
          </Not>
        </Applicable_2>
        <Activate>
          <General RootPath="?GetRegSz(HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\App Paths\chrome.exe,Path)" Flags="Directory" ID="Applicable_1">
            <Query>*.*.*.*</Query>
            <Excluded>?GetFileVersion(%Root%Chrome.exe)</Excluded>
          </General>
          <General RootPath="?GetRegSz(HKLM\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\App Paths\chrome.exe,Path)" Flags="Directory" ID="Applicable_2">
            <Query>*.*.*.*</Query>
            <Excluded>?GetFileVersion(%Root%Chrome.exe)</Excluded>
          </General>
        </Activate>
      </Scan>
    </Item>

    <Item Name="# system 自带Appx应用" Level="2">
      <Description>#this 功能Will 移除所有 system 自带Appx应用，移除后可以exist Windows应用商店重新 download他们. </Description>

      <Scan Work="4">

        <Activate>

    <Item Name="#Installer Table of contents" Level="0">
      <Description>#清理被取代 of msp补丁并减少Installer Table of contents of 大小. </Description>
      <Warning>#(这是一个实验性功能)清理后Will Unable to 卸载被取代 of msprenew ，Do not use this option if you need to uninstall updates. </Warning>
      <Group>#System related</Group>
      <Scan>
        <Applicable>
          <FileExist FilePath="%SystemDrive%\Windows\Installer"/>
        </Applicable>
        <Activate>
          <Custom ProcName="NCInstallerFolderCleanup"/>
        </Activate>
      </Scan>
    </Item>
    
    <Item Name="#损坏 of Appx" Level="2">
      <Description>#清理损坏 of Appx. For example Visual Studio of 通用应用XAML设计器暴力删除临时生成 of 设计器应用，于是会出现大量损坏 of Appx. </Description>
      <Group>#System related</Group>
      <Scan>
        <Applicable>
          <ImageFlags>1</ImageFlags>
          <RegExist Key="HKLM\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Appx" Value="PackageRoot"/>
          <Or>
            <And>
              <Arch>9</Arch>
              <FileVersion FilePath="%0%Config\amd64\NCleaner.dll" Compare=">=">1.0.3.5</FileVersion>
            </And>
            <And>
              <Arch>0</Arch>
              <FileVersion FilePath="%0%Config\x86\NCleaner.dll" Compare=">=">1.0.3.5</FileVersion>
            </And>
            <False/>
          </Or>
        </Applicable>
        <Activate>
          <Custom ProcName="NCCorruptedAppXOnlineCleanup"/>
        </Activate>
      </Scan>
    </Item>

    <Item Name="#NuGet包缓存" Level="2">
      <Description>#引用了NuGet包 of .NETappexist Use Visual Studio生成时产生 of 缓存（尤其是Use WinUI3构建 of app）. </Description>

        </Activate>
      </Scan>

    <Item Name="#CompactOs（较慢）" Level="0">
      <Description>#对单纯读取 of  document进行哈夫曼压缩，exist not 影响性能 of 情况下，显著减少 system 体积. 特别感谢矿工 as well as 所有Compact团队成员none私 of 支持与帮助. </Description>
      <Warning>#Use 后可能导致 some 程序 Unable to function normally 运行甚至让 system Unable to 启动，如果Use 后出现问题，可以exist PE中点击 恢复功能-->撤销Compact. </Warning>
      <Group>#System related</Group>

        <Applicable>

          <Or>

          </Or>

        <Activate>
          <Custom ProcName="DismCompactOs"/>

    <Item Name="#硬链接合并（较慢）" Level="0">
      <Description>#Use 利用NTFS硬链接特性合并所有 document内容相同 of  document. </Description>
      <Warning># some  document被硬链接合并后可能导致相关功能 Unable to function normally Use . </Warning>
      <Group>#System related</Group>
      <Scan Work="40">
        <Activate>
          <Custom ProcName="DismHardLinkMerge"/>
        </Activate>
      </Scan>
    </Item>

    <Item Name="#过期驱动" Level="0">
      <Description>#删除计算机中not Use  of 驱动程序以节省驱动 storage池空间. </Description>
      <Warning>#该功能对于 some 精简 system or手动处理过驱动 of  system 可能发生驱动签名问题. </Warning>
      <Group>#Expired documents</Group>
      <Scan Work="2">
        <Activate>
          <Custom ProcName="DismDriverCleanup"/>
        </Activate>
      </Scan>
    </Item>

    <Item Name="#过期Appx应用" Level="0">
      <Description>#exist Appx应用升级时，会留下老版versions 应用，该功能Will 删除那些not Use  of 老版versions . </Description>
      <Warning>#少数用户报告称Use 后Unable to 打开Appx应用，需want 重新安装Appx应用. </Warning>
      <Group>#Expired documents</Group>
      <Scan Work="4">
        <Applicable>
          <ImageFlags>1</ImageFlags>
          <RegExist Key="HKLM\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Appx" Value="PackageRoot"/>
        </Applicable>
        <Activate>
          <Custom ProcName="DismAppxsCleanup"/>
        </Activate>
      </Scan>
    </Item>

    <Item Name="#Installer基线缓存" Level="0">
      <Description>#Use Installer技术 of 安装程序产生 of 缓存. </Description>
      <Warning>#可能导致卸载Office、VM等app需want 安装包. </Warning>
      <Group>#System related</Group>
      <Scan Work="5">
        <Applicable>
          <FileExist FilePath="%SystemRoot%\Installer\$PatchCache$"/>
          <Not>
            <FileExist FilePath="%SystemDrive%\Program Files\Common Files\Apple"/>
          </Not>
        </Applicable>
        <Activate>
          <General RootPath="%SystemRoot%\Installer\$PatchCache$\"/>
        </Activate>
      </Scan>
    </Item>

    <Item Name="#Office安装源" Level="0">
      <Description>#安装Office后产生 of 安装源，如果unnecessary卸载Office可以考虑删除，删除后能正常安装Officerenew . </Description>
      <Warning>#清理后Will Unable to 卸载只能升级安装or强行删除，Office 2007以下版versions （包含）删除后还影响安装renew . </Warning>
      <Group>#app</Group>
      <ScanCollection>
        <Scan>
          <Applicable>
            <ImageFlags>1</ImageFlags>
            <RegExist Key="HKLM\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office"/>
          </Applicable>
          <Activate>
            <General RootPath="*\" Flags="Directory">
              <Query>MSOCache</Query>
            </General>
          </Activate>
        </Scan>
        <Scan>
          <Applicable>
            <RegExist Key="HKLM\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office"/>
            <FileExist FilePath="%SystemDrive%\MSOCache" />
          </Applicable>
          <Activate>
            <General RootPath="%SystemDrive%\" Flags="Directory">
              <Query>MSOCache</Query>
            </General>
          </Activate>
        </Scan>
      </ScanCollection>
    </Item>

    <Group Name="#task bar相关设置">
      <Item Type="Combo" Name="#Will task bar中 of Cortana Adjust to">
        <Applicable>
          <OSVersion Compare=">=">10.0</OSVersion>
        </Applicable>
        <Current>
          <Dropdown Name="#hide">
            <Applicable>
              <RegExist Key="HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Search" Value="SearchboxTaskbarMode" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="0"/>
            </Applicable>
            <Activate>
              <RegWrite Key="HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Search" Value="SearchboxTaskbarMode" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="0"/>
              <ExplorerNotify Type="Custom" msg="1A" lParam="TraySettings"/>
            </Activate>
          </Dropdown>
          <Dropdown Name="#仅show图标">
            <Applicable>
              <RegExist Key="HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Search" Value="SearchboxTaskbarMode" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="1"/>
            </Applicable>
            <Activate>
              <RegWrite Key="HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Search" Value="SearchboxTaskbarMode" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="1"/>
              <ExplorerNotify Type="Custom" msg="1A" lParam="TraySettings"/>
            </Activate>
          </Dropdown>
          <Dropdown Name="#show搜索框">
            <Applicable>
              <Or>
                <Not>
                  <RegExist Key="HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Search" Value="SearchboxTaskbarMode"/>
                </Not>
                <RegExist Key="HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Search" Value="SearchboxTaskbarMode" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="2"/>
              </Or>
            </Applicable>
            <Activate>
              <RegWrite Key="HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Search" Value="SearchboxTaskbarMode" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="2"/>
              <ExplorerNotify Type="Custom" msg="1A" lParam="TraySettings"/>
            </Activate>
          </Dropdown>
        </Current>

        <Default>
          <Dropdown Name="#hide">
            <Applicable>
              <RegExist Key="HKEY_USERS\DEFAULT\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Search" Value="SearchboxTaskbarMode" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="0"/>
            </Applicable>
            <Activate>
              <RegWrite Key="HKEY_USERS\DEFAULT\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Search" Value="SearchboxTaskbarMode" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="0"/>
            </Activate>
          </Dropdown>
          <Dropdown Name="#仅show图标">
            <Applicable>
              <RegExist Key="HKEY_USERS\DEFAULT\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Search" Value="SearchboxTaskbarMode" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="1"/>
            </Applicable>
            <Activate>
              <RegWrite Key="HKEY_USERS\DEFAULT\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Search" Value="SearchboxTaskbarMode" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="1"/>
            </Activate>
          </Dropdown>

      <Item Type="Combo" Name="#当task bar被占满时">
        <Applicable>
          <OSVersion Compare=">=">6.1</OSVersion>
        </Applicable>
        <Current>
          <Dropdown Name="#Always 合并">
            <Applicable>
              <Or>
                <Not>
                  <RegExist Key="HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\Advanced" Value="TaskbarGlomLevel"/>
                </Not>
                <RegExist Key="HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\Advanced" Value="TaskbarGlomLevel" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="0"/>
              </Or>
            </Applicable>
            <Activate>
              <RegWrite Key="HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\Advanced" Value="TaskbarGlomLevel" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="0"/>
              <ExplorerNotify Type="Custom" msg="1A" lParam="TraySettings"/>
            </Activate>
          </Dropdown>
          <Dropdown Name="#被占满时合并">
            <Applicable>
              <RegExist Key="HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\Advanced" Value="TaskbarGlomLevel" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="1"/>
            </Applicable>
            <Activate>
              <RegWrite Key="HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\Advanced" Value="TaskbarGlomLevel" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="1"/>
              <ExplorerNotify Type="Custom" msg="1A" lParam="TraySettings"/>
            </Activate>

      <Item Type="CheckBox" Name="#closure Quick Start">
        <Applicable>
          <OSVersion Compare=">=">6.2</OSVersion>
          <Not>
            <!--VHD装载、PE system not show-->
            <Or>
              <ImageFlags>40</ImageFlags>
              <ImageFlags>10</ImageFlags>
            </Or>
          </Not>
        </Applicable>
        <System>
          <State>
            <Applicable>
              <Or>
                <!--closure 休眠 or 指定closure Quick Start都认为closure 了Quick Start-->
                <RegExist Key="HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Power" Value="HibernateEnabled" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="0"/>
                <RegExist Key="HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Session Manager\Power" Value="HiberbootEnabled" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="0"/>
              </Or>
            </Applicable>
          </State>
          <True>
            <Warning>#closure Quick Start will result in system 启动速度变慢！</Warning>
            <Activate>
              <RegWrite Key="HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Session Manager\Power" Value="HiberbootEnabled" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="0"/>
            </Activate>
          </True>
          <False>
            <Activate>
              <!--先尝试开启休眠-->
              <ExplorerNotify Type="Cmd" Cmd="powercfg -hibernate on"/>
              <RegWrite Key="HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Power" Value="HibernateEnabled" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="1"/>

              <!--开启Quick Start-->
              <RegWrite Key="HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Session Manager\Power" Value="HiberbootEnabled" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="1"/>
            </Activate>
          </False>
        </System>
      </Item>

            </Applicable>
          </State>
          <True>

          </True>

              <RegWrite Key="HKLM\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows NT\CurrentVersion\Winlogon" Value="ReportBootOk" Type="REG_SZ" Data="1"/>
            </Activate>
          </False>
        </System>
      </Item>

      <Item Type="CheckBox" Name="#Disable WfpDiag.ETL log（by powerxing04）">
        <System>
          <State>
            <Applicable>
              <RegExist Key="HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\BFE\Parameters\Policy\Options" Value="CollectNetEvents" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="0"/>
            </Applicable>
          </State>
          <True>
            <Activate>
              <ExplorerNotify Type="Cmd" Cmd="NETSH WFP SET OPTIONS NETEVENTS=OFF"/>
              <RegWrite Key="HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\BFE\Parameters\Policy\Options" Value="CollectNetEvents" Type="REG_DWORD" Data="0"/>
            </Activate>
          </True>
          <False>
            <Activate>
              <ExplorerNotify Type="Cmd" Cmd="NETSH WFP SET OPTIONS NETEVENTS=ON"/>
              <RegDelete Key="HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Services\BFE\Parameters\Policy\Options" Value="CollectNetEvents"/>
            </Activate>
          </False>
        </System>
      </Item>
